Date: 2024-05-20 15:36:13
Caption: Here’s what big ph*rm@ doesn’t want you to know… Mushrooms are revolutionizing modern medicine! From boosting immunity to sharpening your mind, these versatile fungi offer a bounty of health benefits that are hard to ignore. What really makes them game changers are these key ingredients: - Polysaccharides - complex sugars that stimulate the immune system and have been shown to have anti-inflammatory and antioxidant effects. - Beta-glucans - type of soluble fiber that helps regulate the immune system by binding to immune cells and stimulate them to attack invading pathogens, while also reducing inflammation in the body. - Active hexose correlated compound - nutritional product extracted from a variety of mushrooms that is commonly used to prevent and treat cancer. It contains a mixture of the polysaccharides, amino acids and minerals. I have experienced the amazing benefits first hand. My go-tos are @real_mushrooms and @thegeniusbrand. For more on mushrooms, drop the words “Mushroom guide” for my FREE in depth guide on the subject Have you also had an amazing experience with using mushrooms? #medicinalmushroom #fungi #fungilove #mushroomlove #mushroom #mushrooms

Caption: Con esta maravillosa especie (Atheniella adonis) y la manifestación más linda que he visto de ellas hasta ahora, les dejo el afiche de nuestra expedición fotográfica "Costa fúngica del Maule", la cual se realizará los días 14, 15, y 16 de Junio. Así es, serán 3 días de exploración intensiva en busca de toda la biodiversidad posible, pero por supuesto con enfoque especial en el mítico Reino Fungi y sus extravagantes y magníficos representantes.😍🍄 Además, podrás aprender todos los secretos para lograr mejores fotografías, a través de la experiencia. A todos los fanáticos de los hongos, y a los que quieren conocer más de ellos, es tiempo de ponerse en #ModoMicelio y disfrutar desde nuestros hogares las entretenidas actividades de la quinta versión de @FungiFest. Todos los años, este festival se celebra en Valdivia, pero esta versión se podrá disfrutar de manera online. La programación del festival incluye charlas, talleres, concursos y conversatorios sobre gastronomía fúngica, recolección, cultivo de hongos, ciencia y cultura. Todo esto bajo la compañía del “Profesor Entoloma”, el personaje inspirado en el hongo oficial del FungiFest 2020, el Entoloma necopinatum. Caption: Here are various stages of growth of Mycena manipularis (syn.=Filoboletus/Favolaschia manipularis) aka “Luminous Porecaps”. While these are bioluminescent - I show what they look like in daylight. Note: the second image has a different species in the mix, as Luminous Porecaps (as the name suggests-have pores, not gills). It’s interesting to see how some start out with a dark tan cap and then fade and lighten to a milky, translucent white as they age.

Labels:
Natural material Bryophyte Frost Moss Liverworts
Date: 2024-05-31 21:30:36
Caption: ✨𝗜𝗻 𝘁𝗵𝗲 𝗺𝘆𝘅’✨ Imaginez un organisme à la croisée des règnes animal et végétal, qui se développe comme une plante mais se déplace comme un animal. C’est 𝗖𝗲𝗿𝗮𝘁𝗶𝗼𝗺𝘆𝘅𝗮 𝗳𝗿𝘂𝘁𝗶𝗰𝘂𝗹𝗼𝘀𝗮, un myxomycète. Il se présente sous une forme étonnante, rappelant un corail miniature ou de minuscules stalactites. Ses ramifications blanches se développent sur les bois morts, formant des structures délicates et complexes. Ces ramifications, mesurant jusqu’à 4 millimètres de long, arborent une apparence veloutée due à la présence de spores à leur surface. Loin d’être statique, Ceratiomyxa fruticulosa suit un cycle de vie semblable aux autres myxomycètes. Tout commence sous forme de spores microscopiques dispersées dans l’air. Lorsqu’elles atterrissent sur un substrat favorable, généralement du bois mort humide, elles germent et se transforment en cellules amiboïdes flagellées dotées d’une capacité de mouvement étonnante puis fusionnent pour former un plasmodium, une masse visqueuse multinucléée. Le plasmodium se développe en rampant sur le bois, engloutissant les bactéries et les champignons qui lui servent de nourriture. Au bout d’un certain temps, le plasmodium se transforme en structures reproductrices appelées sporanges. Ces sporanges libèrent à leur tour de nouvelles spores, perpétuant ainsi le cycle de vie de cet organisme étonnant. En décomposant le bois mort, il contribue au recyclage des nutriments dans le sol. J’imagine que le temps extrêmement pluvieux de cette année favorise son apparition nettement plus remarquée actuellement que d’habitude. (Photos en studio 😀) #funghi#champignons#mushrooms#pilze#foret#forest#forestlover#fungis #nature#naturelovers#macronature#beautyofnature #nature#naturalists#biodiversity#naturalistes#wildlife #guidenature #mycologue#mycologie#mycology #photo#photooftheday#picoftheday#natureart #beautyfull#myxomycetes #inthemyxs

Caption: A Fungi Nomade Fest 🍄‍🟫 Last week’s weather was all over the place. From blazing sun and pouring rain, to even hail on the same day! Even with harsh weather changes like these, there is one #supercrop that can grow year-round in a controlled indoor environment, and still be incredibly #sustainable 🌱 @ilfungoeclettico 👀‼️ Considering the drastic changes of temperature in one day, we wanted to satisfy both warm and cold cravings ✨ For the zuppa di giorno, @pinasiotto went with a twist on the iconic #Pancotto but with fungi, chives, asparagi, and a generous sprinkle of Parmigiano 💛 I took the lead with a Fungiche, a #plantbased twist on a #PeruvianCeviche 🇵🇪 Slow-cooked #Pleurotus Florida marinated in tomato water, red onion, lemon and orange juice 🍊 For a sweet and smoky taste, we added charred bell peppers, and finished with a celery, ginger, and cilantro “leche de tigre” 🐯 🧆 As a bonus, of course I got to try their Lentil Falafel with a cucumber pico de gallo and smoked eggplant sauce Once again, I am so thankful for this empowering hub that continues to encourage me to let go of fears and just have fun(gi) 🤣💜 @cristina_fiorese #pastonomade #pastonomadebologna #ilfungoeclettico #urbanmushrooms #urbanfungi #fungigrowing #fungifreaks #vegetariancooking #vegetariancuisine #veganceviche #cevichevegano #cevichevegetariano #fungiculture #fungicultura #pleurotusflorida

Nature Fungus Mushroom Ingredient Close-up Brown Groundcover Edible mushroom Agaricaceae Macro photography
Date: 2024-06-03 13:03:14
Caption: 🆔Inosperma erubescens (Inocybe erubescens) 👉🏽Deadly Fibrecap, brick-red tear mushroom 👉🏽Ziegelroter Risspilz 👉🏽变红丝盖伞 (reddening silk top umbrella) 🌟 The brick-red splitting mushroom (Inocybe erubescens) can be found on forest paths, in parks, or in deciduous forests, especially under beech or linden trees on calcareous, nutrient-rich soils. 🌳🍃 The fruit bodies of this mushroom appear from spring/early summer until late autumn. 🌸🍂 🌟 磚紅裂褶菇（Inocybe erubescens）可以在林間小徑、公園或闊葉林中找到，特別是在含鈣、富營養的土壤中的山毛櫸或菩提樹下。🌳🍃 這種蘑菇的子實體從春季/初夏到晚秋出現。🌸🍂 ⚠️ **WARNING:** Inocybe erubescens contains a potentially fatal dose of the toxin muscarine. ⚠️😱 However, its deadly toxicity depends on the amount consumed; a small piece might not cause severe illness, but eating an entire mushroom can be fatal. 🍄☠️ ⚠️ **警告：** 磚紅裂褶菇含有致命劑量的毒素——毒蕈鹼。⚠️😱 然而，其致命毒性取決於攝入量；少量可能不會引起嚴重疾病，但食用整個蘑菇可能致命。🍄☠️ 📚 All mushroom guidebooks and mushroom hunters advise against consuming any members of the Inocybaceae family! ❌🚫 📚 所有的蘑菇指南書和蘑菇獵人都建議不要食用任何Inocybaceae科的成員！❌🚫 Today, when I discovered these Inocybe mushrooms in the village next to some linden trees, I had to lie down on the ground to take pictures and examine them carefully. 📸👀 This was when a car stopped right behind me, and a man got out to ask if everything was okay. 🚗💨 I felt a bit awkward but reassured him that I was fine. 😅 It was heartening to see that people care if someone is spread out on the ground, regardless of the reason. ❤️🙏 今天，當我在村子裡的一些菩提樹旁發現這些裂褶菇時，我不得不躺在地上拍照並仔細檢查它們。📸👀 就在這時，一輛車停在我身後，一位男士下車問我是否一切正常。🚗💨 我感到有點尷尬，但我向他保證我沒事。😅 看到人們關心無論何種原因躺在地上的人，這讓我感到很暖心。❤️🙏 #InocybeErubescens 🍄🌿🕵️‍♂️ I tried some microscopy on this one. 🔬🧬 Image one shows cheilocystidia, and in between the two big cheilocystidia is a basidium with two sterigmata (they look like tiny antennas). 🧫🔍 The second microscopy image shows spores, which are oval to almond-shaped. I used Melzer's reagent to stain the sample. 🧪📸 Oh my, microscopy terminology is really hard! Definitely need to catch up. 😅 In case you know any of the terms in Chinese, please feel free to comment. Cheilozystidia 緣擔孢子囊 Basidia 擔子 Sterigmata 擔梗

Yellow Orange Fungus Macro photography Mushroom
Date: 2024-05-26 11:18:21
Caption: Growing a new fungus is always interesting. This is Cordyceps militaris #cordycepsmilitaris a fungi that until recently was not allowed to be grown here in Australia. Now we can legally grow this, I was curious to give it a go - especially after investing so much time into trying to grow Cordyceps gunnii, unsuccessfully! Not my best grow! And I have been watching lots of US growers really get to dial these in to be an art. But I grew these on white rice with no nutrients to start out so I could get an idea of growth, yield, and other characteristics that may help later! One big hint, don't try to grow these when it is hot without cooling! #guerrillamycology #fungiculture #🍄 #fungi #fungus #funghi #hongos #myceliumrunning #radicalmycology #radmycology #thinkfungi #mycology #mycophile #mycophilia #mycelium #mushrooms #myceliumrunning #myceliumnetwork #myceliummood #cordyceps #cordycepsmilitaris #cordycepsgunnii #introducedfungi #notnativefungi #notwildfungi #ethnomycology #entheogenicfungi #fungiphotography #mushroomphotography

Date: 2024-05-26 11:18:21
Caption: Growing a new fungus is always interesting. This is Cordyceps militaris #cordycepsmilitaris a fungi that until recently was not allowed to be grown here in Australia. Now we can legally grow this, I was curious to give it a go - especially after investing so much time into trying to grow Cordyceps gunnii, unsuccessfully! Not my best grow! And I have been watching lots of US growers really get to dial these in to be an art. But I grew these on white rice with no nutrients to start out so I could get an idea of growth, yield, and other characteristics that may help later! One big hint, don't try to grow these when it is hot without cooling! #guerrillamycology #fungiculture #🍄 #fungi #fungus #funghi #hongos #myceliumrunning #radicalmycology #radmycology #thinkfungi #mycology #mycophile #mycophilia #mycelium #mushrooms #myceliumrunning #myceliumnetwork #myceliummood #cordyceps #cordycepsmilitaris #cordycepsgunnii #introducedfungi #notnativefungi #notwildfungi #ethnomycology #entheogenicfungi #fungiphotography #mushroomphotography

Caption: Growing a new fungus is always interesting. This is Cordyceps militaris #cordycepsmilitaris a fungi that until recently was not allowed to be grown here in Australia. Pink Graphic design
Date: 2024-05-29 20:56:52
Caption: Glosario para el Antropoceno | Funga Otoño es temporada de hongos. En esta época es posible observar su estructura macroscópica, que no es más que su cuerpo reproductivo. Es por esta razón que hemos hecho un glosario especial para este reino, tan importante en el engranaje de la vida. Hasta el siglo pasado, se los consideraba como parte del reino Plantae. Sin embargo, estos se acercan más a los animales que a las plantas, aunque no encajan en ninguno de los dos reinos. Los hongos son la base de la vida, pues construyen los puentes entre todos los ciclos biológicos. Así por ejemplo: son los que contribuyen a hacer el reciclaje de nutrientes en la naturaleza, con sus micorrizas son protagonistas de las asociaciones interespecie y el intercambio de nutrientes, muchos tienen un valor gastronómico relevante y otros, incluso son importantes enteógenos, que nos ayudan a elevar nuestro estado de conciencia. Alimentos, medicinas, transformadores de la materia, mágicos habitantes de los bosques y otros tantos ecosistemas, los hongos merecen su espacio en la clasificación de la biodiversidad. La incorporación del término Funga nos invita, entonces, a apreciar y proteger el mundo de estos seres únicos. 🍄 Si te gusta este contenido, te invitamos a guardar, compartir y darle me gusta. Encuentra más gráficas similares en endemico.org/visuales #revistaendemico #funga #reinofungi #hongos #micorrizas #hifas #florafaunayfungi #visualesendemico

Text Font Graphic design Publication
Date: 2024-05-29 20:56:52
Caption: Glosario para el Antropoceno | Funga Otoño es temporada de hongos. En esta época es posible observar su estructura macroscópica, que no es más que su cuerpo reproductivo. Es por esta razón que hemos hecho un glosario especial para este reino, tan importante en el engranaje de la vida. Hasta el siglo pasado, se los consideraba como parte del reino Plantae. Sin embargo, estos se acercan más a los animales que a las plantas, aunque no encajan en ninguno de los dos reinos. Los hongos son la base de la vida, pues construyen los puentes entre todos los ciclos biológicos. Así por ejemplo: son los que contribuyen a hacer el reciclaje de nutrientes en la naturaleza, con sus micorrizas son protagonistas de las asociaciones interespecie y el intercambio de nutrientes, muchos tienen un valor gastronómico relevante y otros, incluso son importantes enteógenos, que nos ayudan a elevar nuestro estado de conciencia. Alimentos, medicinas, transformadores de la materia, mágicos habitantes de los bosques y otros tantos ecosistemas, los hongos merecen su espacio en la clasificación de la biodiversidad. La incorporación del término Funga nos invita, entonces, a apreciar y proteger el mundo de estos seres únicos. 🍄 Si te gusta este contenido, te invitamos a guardar, compartir y darle me gusta. Encuentra más gráficas similares en endemico.org/visuales #revistaendemico #funga #reinofungi #hongos #micorrizas #hifas #florafaunayfungi #visualesendemico

Date: 2024-03-12 11:37:56
Caption: Aquele post para salvar📌 Os fungicidas desempenham um papel crucial no manejo dos fungos, responsáveis por aproximadamente 65% das enfermidades que afetam as plantações agrícolas. É fundamental compreender suas categorias para planejar sua aplicação de forma eficaz, prevenindo, por exemplo, o desenvolvimento de resistência a pesticidas. Podemos utilizar pelo menos 8 critérios distintos para classificar os fungicidas agrícolas, a saber: Grupo químico Principio de controle Mobilidade Espectro de ação Mecanismo de ação Potencial de periculosidade ambiental Toxicologia Formulações Quer liberar o seu acesso ao combo de fitopatologia com 52 mapas mentais da matéria? Yellow Fungus Macro photography Algae
Date: 2024-06-05 16:12:10
Caption: ℹ️ Dünnsporiges Kranzbecherchen (Vibrissea flavorirens) Vibrissea flavorirens ist ein Bewohner sauberer Bäche, Quellsümpfe usw. Es besiedelt, oft sehr zahlreich, entrindete, harte Laubholzäste, die ständig von fließendem Wasser umspült werden. Die Apothecien werden ca 2-3mm groß, sind kurz gestielt und haben einen charakteristischen, zahnradähnlich gekerbten Rand. Die dünnen Fäden, die auf dem letzten Bild im Hintergrund herumfliegen, sind die, mit bis 250μm Länge, riesigen Sporen. 🗓️ 26.05.2024 🍴 ungenießbar 🚩 Rote Liste (DE): Vorwarnliste #vibrisseaflavovirens #dünnsporigeskranzbecherchen #pilze #fungi #mushrooms #mycology #nature #pilzfotografie #mushroomphotography #pilzesammeln #pilzesuchen #mushroomhunting #mushroomsofınstagram #fungiofinstagram #fungilove #fantasticfungi #fungifreaks #makrofotografie #macrophotography #forestfinds #darmstadt #spessart #rotelistepilze

Caption: ℹ️ Dünnsporiges Kranzbecherchen (Vibrissea flavorirens) Vibrissea flavorirens ist ein Bewohner sauberer Bäche, Quellsümpfe usw. Es besiedelt, oft sehr zahlreich, entrindete, harte Laubholzäste, die ständig von fließendem Wasser umspült werden. Die Apothecien werden ca 2-3mm groß, sind kurz gestielt und haben einen charakteristischen, zahnradähnlich gekerbten Rand. Date: 2024-05-28 15:14:59
Caption: 🧚🏼‍♂️ Gomita del bosque (Guepiniopsis alpina) Es un tipo de hongo de color amarillo o anaranjado cuando es joven y rojizo en su etapa adulta. Tiene un cuerpo fructífero o carpóforo pequeño de contextura gelatinosa (juventud) y coriácea (madurez) 🍄🤏 En la fotografía tome una rama caída de madera muerta que estaba en el suelo del bosque del género Nothofagus en @parquetricahue en la región del Maule 🌳🍁🌿🍂 📍Amplia distribución desde la IV región hasta la Patagonia chilena y Argentina Austral 🏞️🏔️ 🍽️ No tiene valor gastronómico #micologia #hongosdechile #hongossilvestres #mushrooms #guepiniopsisalpina #bosque #parquetricahue #fungicultura

Caption: Aquele post para salvar📌 Os fungicidas desempenham um papel crucial no manejo dos fungos, responsáveis por aproximadamente 65% das enfermidades que afetam as plantações agrícolas. É fundamental compreender suas categorias para planejar sua aplicação de forma eficaz, prevenindo, por exemplo, o desenvolvimento de resistência a pesticidas. Podemos utilizar pelo menos 8 critérios distintos para classificar os fungicidas agrícolas, a saber: Grupo químico Principio de controle Mobilidade Espectro de ação Mecanismo de ação Potencial de periculosidade ambiental Toxicologia Formulações Quer liberar o seu acesso ao combo de fitopatologia com 52 mapas mentais da matéria? Yellow Fungus Natural material Macro photography Algae
Date: 2024-06-05 16:12:10
Caption: ℹ️ Dünnsporiges Kranzbecherchen (Vibrissea flavorirens) Vibrissea flavorirens ist ein Bewohner sauberer Bäche, Quellsümpfe usw. Es besiedelt, oft sehr zahlreich, entrindete, harte Laubholzäste, die ständig von fließendem Wasser umspült werden. Die Apothecien werden ca 2-3mm groß, sind kurz gestielt und haben einen charakteristischen, zahnradähnlich gekerbten Rand. Die dünnen Fäden, die auf dem letzten Bild im Hintergrund herumfliegen, sind die, mit bis 250μm Länge, riesigen Sporen. 🗓️ 26.05.2024 🍴 ungenießbar 🚩 Rote Liste (DE): Vorwarnliste #vibrisseaflavovirens #dünnsporigeskranzbecherchen #pilze #fungi #mushrooms #mycology #nature #pilzfotografie #mushroomphotography #pilzesammeln #pilzesuchen #mushroomhunting #mushroomsofınstagram #fungiofinstagram #fungilove #fantasticfungi #fungifreaks #makrofotografie #macrophotography #forestfinds #darmstadt #spessart #rotelistepilze

Symmetry Design Symbol Graphics Graphic design
Date: 2021-07-24 21:19:36
Caption: Happy full moon #mushroomlovers 🌑🌘🌗🌖🌕🌔🌓🌒🌑 #Repost from @symbiiotica 🍄 How do lunar cycles influence the cycles of fungi? Considering the fact that lunar gravity influences every being on this planet, especially water bodies and those with water-based bodies (most of life), and considering the fact that most mushrooms are > 90% water… it’s almost certain that the moons influences plays SOME role in fungal fruitings, behaviors and expressions. Many Indigenous cultures that have deeply rooted ethnomycological history, especially those of the northern hemisphere in Scandinavia and Siberia, claim that fruitings of ground-dwelling, fleshy macrofungi occur in greater abundance on the full moon. Since the moons gravity pulls the terrestrial tides (ground water) further up to the surface of the soil on full moons and even more so on new moons, it would make sense that lunar events have a direct effect on fruiting of certain species. But for now the exact knowing of these influences stays happily shrouded in mystery. What the moons exact role is in fungal cycles, we just don’t really know. And maybe we’ll never know. And that’s okay. ~ Here is a rendition of the basic life cycle of a basidiomycete mushroom cycling with the lunar phases. From my perspective, I’ve matched the different energetic expressions of the mushroom life cycle with the associated energetic expressions of the lunar cycle. From full; the biggest, boldest, brightest expression of the mature, sporulating fruiting body, to new; the deep, dark inquisitive phase of underground, rhizospheric mycelial navigation, and back again. In the center is the Elder Futhark Norse Rune, Inguz. The Elder Futhark runic alphabet is said to be the most ancient form of the many Indigenous writing systems from my Scandinavian ancestral lineages(s). Inguz or “the God, Ing” is the rune of fertility and new beginnings, marking a new phase of life. Also interpreted as a seed, the birthing of a new idea or life form. The shape also represents a doorway, the portal to the astral planes.

Caption: スジオチバタケ祭り会場のすぐ脇で #おいしいきのこ 🍄が今年も出てた🤗 #オイルパスタ 🍝で美味しく戴きました😋 #ハラタケ #原茸 #fieldmushrooms #agaricuscampestris #天然きのこ料理 #自炊記録 #男の料理 #ひとりごはん #🍄 #きのこ #キノコ #天然きのこ #天然キノコ #きのこ狩り #キノコ狩り #きのこ好き #きのこパトロール #mushroom #mushrooms #mushroomlover #mushroomphotography #wildmushrooms #mushroomhunting #fungiphotography #fungi #fungus ⚠️きのこの食味記述について 筆者個人の感想もしくは一般的な評価と筆者が認識しているものです😄 ⚠️天然食材を食べることは… 食中毒のリスクがあることを十二分に認識して自己責任で楽しんでいます。種の同定に100％の自信が無いきのこや山菜は食べません。食用とされる天然きのこや山菜であっても体質・体調や食べる量、下処理や調理方法の誤りで中毒を起こすこともあることを留意してください🙏
